## flask
### prefix
#### FlaskEffectNotRemovedOnFullMana1
```
 {
    "adds_tags": [],
    "domain": "flask",
    "generation_type": "prefix",
    "generation_weights": [],
    "grants_buff": {},
    "grants_effects": [],
    "group": "FlaskEffectNotRemovedOnFullMana",
    "is_essence_only": false,
    "name": "Enduring",
    "required_level": 16,
    "spawn_weights": [
        {
            "tag": "utility_flask",
            "weight": 0
        },
        {
            "tag": "life_flask",
            "weight": 0
        },
        {
            "tag": "default",
            "weight": 1000
        }
    ],
    "stats": [
        {
            "id": "local_flask_effect_not_removed_at_full_mana",
            "max": 1,
            "min": 1
        },
        {
            "id": "local_flask_duration_+%",
            "max": -25,
            "min": -25
        }
    ],
    "type": "FlaskEffectNotRemovedOnFullMana"
}
```
